<script language="JavaScript">
	javascript:window.history.forward(1);
	
	//Openes popup window for a given url, width, height and window name
	//The address bar and toolbar are not shown in this popup.
	function openSizeWindow(url,width,height,name)
	{
		var ht = screen.height;
		var wdth = screen.width;
		var newWidth = width;
		var newHeight = height;
		var lft = (wdth / 2) - (newWidth / 2);
		var tp = (ht / 2) - (newHeight / 2);
		var w = window.open (url, name, "location=no,screen x=200,screen y=200,toolbar=no,directories=no,status=no, menubar=no,scrollbars=yes,resizable=yes,copyhistory=no,left="+ lft + ",top="+ tp +",width="+ newWidth  +",height="+ newHeight);
	}
	
	//Text search box is cleared, when the search button is clicked 
	//and if the text box has the words 'Search by keywords'
	//Changed for search by ref number. cc3203
	function clearBox(comp)
	{
		if((comp.name == "txtKeyWord"))
		{
			if(document.frmQuickVacancySearch.txtKeyWord.value == "Search by keywords")
			{
					//set the keyword textbox empty
					document.frmQuickVacancySearch.txtKeyWord.value = "";
			}
		}else if(comp.name =="txtJSCode"){
			if(document.frmQuickVacancySearch.txtJSCode.value == "Search by Job Ref Number"){
				document.frmQuickVacancySearch.txtJSCode.value = "";
			}
		}else if(comp.name == "btnSearch" || comp.name == "chkGovt" || comp.name == "chkNGO" || comp.name == "chkParttime" || comp.name == "chkWalkin"){
			if(document.frmQuickVacancySearch.txtKeyWord.value == "Search by keywords"){
				document.frmQuickVacancySearch.txtKeyWord.value = "";
			}
			
			if(document.frmQuickVacancySearch.txtJSCode.value == "Search by Job Ref Number"){
				document.frmQuickVacancySearch.txtJSCode.value = "";
			}
		}
	}
	
	//resize panels etc.
	function resizePanels() {
		width = document.documentElement.clientWidth;
		
		//set the width of the main area where all hot jobs gets displayed
		$("#content-main").width(width - 160);

		//sets the width of a single section where a hot job is displayed
		$(".job-column").width((width - 200)/4);	//changed 3 to 4 dilan	
	}
	
	$(document).ready(function(){
		
		//re-set the sizes of the panels/divs upon window resize
		resizePanels();
		
		//re-set the sizes of the panels/divs upon window resize
		$(window).bind('resize', function() { 
				resizePanels();
		});

  	});
  	
	var i = Math.floor(Math.random()*1);
	var banner = new Array();
	var duration = new Array();
	var timeId = 0;
	var isDefault = false;
	function initiateBanner(){
		
		
			banner[0] = "<a href='../admin/BannerServlet?c=BAN0000000467' target='_blank'><img src='banner/EXT0000000069/BAN0000000467.gif' border='0' height='87' class='banner-link' /></a>";
			duration[0] = "7";
			
		

				
	}
	
	function rotateBanner(){

		if(banner[i] == null){
			banner[i] = "";
			}
		document.getElementById("topRightBanner").innerHTML = banner[i];
		timeId = setTimeout("rotateBanner()", duration[i]*1000);
			if(i == banner.length - 1){
				i = 0;
			}else{
				i++;
			}

			if(isDefault){
				clearTimeout(timeId);
			}
		
		}
	
</script>
